The Subject's first public appearance — dispatched by Department H to intercept the Hulk crossing into Canadian territory after the Wendigo affair — is operationally significant beyond its publication-history novelty. The fight specifics: he engages a vastly stronger opponent with no realistic expectation of victory, refuses tactical withdrawal, sustains injuries the healing factor must work hard to close, and disengages only on orders. The pattern is the *operational signature* he will carry into the X-Men: *threat-overload does not trigger flight; it triggers escalation*. The Hulk encounter is the first public exhibition of the inverted survival reflex that the workup names — the trained recklessness toward his own body, predicated on the healing factor's reliability, with a low-grade lifelong wish for an ending that will stick.

### The growing dissatisfaction

Through 1974, the file shows mounting friction with Department H: refusal of certain assignments, unauthorized side activity, two recorded incidents of berserker-state activation during training exercises (no fatalities, narrowly), and an increasing pattern of solitary wilderness absences between deployments. The Hudsons cover for him; James, in particular, manages upward to keep the Subject from being reassigned to deeper-classification roles that would *re-enact Weapon X conditions*. The Subject is aware of this protection and resents it slightly even as he depends on it. The relationship to Hudson is the first instance of his mature *authority-pattern* (workup §5, interpersonal): insubordinate by default, compliant only under earned trust, then loyal past the point of his own interest.

---

## VI. The Threshold: Xavier's Recruitment (1975)

### The defection

Charles Xavier's recruitment of the Subject (*Giant-Size X-Men* #1, May 1975) is, *behaviorally read*, another flight from a handler. Xavier offers what Department H cannot: removal from Canadian-government jurisdiction, a peer cohort of mutants, a stated mission of protection rather than en


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

## Frame and scope

This section covers the subject's life from approximately the dissolution of the Utopia/post-Schism configuration through the Krakoan settlement, its collapse, and the Fall-of-X / From-the-Ashes present. It is the densest behavioral period in the file because the institutional context — sovereign mutant statehood, resurrection-as-protocol, parliamentary office, then sovereignty's violent collapse and personal exile — externalizes nearly every internal pattern catalogued in Sections 1–4. The subject's CPTSD/dissociative architecture is, in this era, *legible at the institutional scale*: you can read his disorder off the policy.

---

## A. The Schism → Jean Grey School period (Aaron, 2011–2015)

After the Schism with Cyclops (*X-Men: Schism* #1–5, 2011), the subject formally rejects the Utopia-era militarization of mutant youth and reopens the Westchester campus as the **Jean Grey School for Higher Learning** (*Wolverine and the X-Men* #1, 2011, Aaron/Bachalo). This is the cleanest single behavioral datum of the decade: presented with a binary between *standing army* and *school*, he chooses school, and accepts the headmaster role — an office he is by temperament unsuited for, which is precisely why he takes it. The mentorship-of-the-young drive (Section 3, "compensatory mechanisms — positive") is here promoted to *vocation* and *legal title*.

Granular markers from this period:

- He keeps an office, signs paperwork, fundraises (the Hellfire Club / Kade Kilgore arc, *Wolverine and the X-Men* #1–8): behaviorally, sustained desk-tolerance, novel for him.
- He retains private quarters in the boathouse / a back-of-property cabin pattern carried over from Xavier-era habit: he sleeps near, not in, the institution he runs.
- Cigar consumption observed indoors despite his own no-smoking rule for students — a small chronic rule-of-self-exemption consistent with his lifelong stance toward institutions he himself heads.
- Drinking moves from bar-rooms to a private bottle in the office (Aaron run, recurrent panels). The intake is steady rather than binge — a maintenance-dose pattern, consistent with anxiolytic self-medication rather than recreational use.
- The relationship with Idie Okonkwo, Quentin Quire, Kid Omega, Genesis (Evan Sabahnur — the cloned child-Apocalypse) is paradigmatic: he attaches most reliably to the children the institution is most afraid of. Genesis in particular reactivates his *Death-of-Apocalypse* identity-fragment (Section 1, late-career hardening) and he handles it by *raising the child*, i.e., reparative inversion.

Concurrently he continues an Avengers tour of duty (Bendis, Remender) — the *two-team* pattern (school by day, Avengers strike-team by night) is a structural splitting: the regulated paternal mode and the discharge mode kept in separate institutions to prevent contamination. This works for roughly three years.

---

## B. *Death of Wolverine* (Soule/McNiven, 2014) — the loss of the healing factor and the adamantium drowning

The Microverse-derived virus suppresses his healing factor. For the first time in the period covered by the file he is *mortal in real time*. Behavioral observations during the terminal arc:

- He sets his affairs (visits to Lady Deathstrike, Sabretooth, Kitty, Daken, Laura) — a deliberate *closure tour*. The order of visits is itself a diagnostic ranking of his attachments: enemies first (ritual debts), then the chosen children.
- He refuses to pop the claws against Cornelius's experimental subjects, choosing to die by adamantium pour rather than kill the captive surrogates. He dies *suffocating in metal*, which I note in Section 2 as the literalization of his iatrogenic somatic load: the instrument of his torture becomes the instrument of his death. He has, in effect, been dying of Weapon X for forty years; the manner of death finalizes a metaphor.
- The death pose — encased, arms partially extended — is consistent with someone who chose to face the pour rather than flee it. There is no behavioral indication of panic in the final sequence. This is a man for whom death has been a fantasy of cessation since at least 1907.

A roughly four-year publication interval follows in which the subject is dead-in-amber, displayed as a statue at the school. The behavioral file is suspended; the *institutional* effect is significant — the school, the X-Men, Laura (who takes the name and the role: *All-New Wolverine*, Taylor/Lopez, 2015), and Daken all reorganize around the absence. Laura's tenure as Wolverine during this interval is, retroactively, the most successful piece of the subject's parenting: she does the job *better regulated* than he did, which is itself a measure of what he taught.

---

## C. Return, Persephone, and the re-implantation of triggers (*Return of Wolverine*, Soule, 2018–2019)

He returns warm-bodied, with **fresh kill-triggers implanted by Persephone**, partial amnesia, the claws episodically running hot (heated to glowing — an unexplained somatic novelty consistent with the regeneration-recompilation). Diagnostically this is the cycle re-asserted: *another agent has overwritten him while he was unconscious.* The structural fact noted in Section 1 — "the cycle is structural, not narrative" — is here demonstrated within a single publication year of his resurrection. He cannot remain un-tampered-with.

Behavioral residue carried forward: he treats his own consciousness, for the next several arcs, as **provisionally his**. He checks his hands. He asks others (Kitty, Nightcrawler) to tell him if he is "acting like himself." This is a clinically appropriate response to confirmed dissociative-identity-alteration history and represents, in fact, the most psychologically mature stretch of his life — the disorder is finally being *named by the patient*.

---

## D. Krakoa — the institutional era (Hickman et al., *House of X / Powers of X* through *Inferno*, 2019–2022)

The mutant nation-state is founded. The subject accepts a seat on the **Quiet Council of Krakoa**, occupying one of the four "Autumn" thrones beside Kurt Nightcrawler. The Council seat is, behaviorally, a profound development: he votes on laws. He does not, in the prior century of evidence, *vote on laws.* That he tolerates parliamentary process indicates the school-era desk-tolerance has consolidated into something like civic capacity — though always with the same private-cabin sleeping pattern, in his case Krakoan **"The Boneyard"** retreat and the floating bar **The Green Lagoon**.

The Green Lagoon (introduced *X-Men* vol. 5 #6, Hickman/Yu) is the most operationally diagnostic location of this entire period. He establishes, with Magneto and a rotating cast, a bar where mutants who *cannot get drunk on Krakoan biology* drink imported off-island liquor specifically engineered to bypass their resistances. The subject is the bar's most reliable patron. Read this clinically: in a utopia that has technically solved death, he engineers a chemical pathway to *the brief unconsciousness alcohol used to provide.* The anxiolytic need persists in paradise; the drive is internal, not situational. This is the single most clarifying behavioral fact about him in the Krakoan era.

The **Resurrection Protocols** (Five-driven re-incarnation from backup) transform his lifelong somatic recklessness into *policy.* He dies and is reborn — on-page — multiple times in the Krakoan period (*X Lives / X Deaths of Wolverine*, Percy, 2022; X-Force missions; various Hellfire Gala incidents). Each resurrection is a controlled iteration of the Weapon X awakening — *naked, on a slab, attended by handlers.* That he tolerates this and uses it as a tactical resource indicates either: (a) genuine integration of the trauma into a usable schema, or — my read — (b) the institutionalization of the dissociation, where the *system* now performs the splitting that his psyche used to perform alone. Krakoa is, for him, an exoskeleton for his disorder. It works, until it doesn't.

Concurrent threads in the Krakoan period:

- **X-Force** (Percy, 2019–2024): black-ops, intelligence-and-assassination cell, the violent discharge institution kept parallel to his Council/civic role. The Schism-era *two-team* splitting is reproduced exactly at Krakoan scale. Beast as handler in this configuration represents a *new* destabilizer — Beast's covert atrocities, when surfaced, will require the subject to kill or neutralize a longstanding friend, and the file records his discomfort across the run.
- **The relationship with Jean Grey and Cyclops** is reframed by the editorial decision that the three live in adjoining quarters in the **Summer House on the Moon** (*X-Men* vol. 5 #1, Hickman/Yu). This is the most novel interpersonal data of the entire decade. The Rose/Mariko/Itsu *idealize-then-withdraw* pattern (Section 3) is, for the first time, replaced by a stable, openly acknowledged, non-exclusive configuration. The pattern's *interruption* is itself the datum: with a partner whose own marital configuration removes the prediction "she will die because of me," he can sustain proximity. The pattern was always *predictive,* not *desirous.* Given an arrangement in which the catastrophe model does not apply, intimacy holds.
- **Daken** is brought to Krakoa and seated at the same table. Father-son contact is more sustained in this period than in the entire prior century. It is not warm, but it is present. Reparative across generations.
- **Laura** continues, as X-23 / Wolverine / Talon, in adjacent missions. The two operate occasionally as a paired unit. He defers to her on operational calls more often than he initiates — observably the most regulated peer-with-adult-child relationship in his record.
- **Sabretooth** is exiled to the Pit by Council vote, which the subject co-authors. This sets up the *Sabretooth War* arc (Percy, 2023–2024). Note the prediction in Section 5 — "Creed's permanent removal might be more destabilizing than his presence" — is *tested* by Sabretooth's escape and revenge campaign, which inflicts heavier personal losses on the subject than nearly any prior Creed encounter. The destabilizer was, indeed, load-bearing.

---

## E. *X Lives / X Deaths of Wolverine* (Percy, 2022) and the *Sabretooth War* (Percy, 2023–2024)

In *X Lives / X Deaths*, Omega Red and the Phalanx-affiliated future-cabal targeting him produce a sequence of forced timeline-jumps, programmed assassinations, and recursive resurrections in which the subject is — again — used as a weapon by parties unknown to himself at the point of action. The diagnostic content: *even on Krakoa, even with institutional supports, even with the Council seat, he can still be overwritten.* The Weapon X template is not a historical event but a recurring vulnerability.

The *Sabretooth War* arc (*Wolverine* vol. 7 #41–50) is the inflection point of his late-Krakoan behavior. Creed returns with a pack — including Wild Child, Lady Deathstrike alt-iterations — and inflicts grievous losses on the subject's small attachments (Jubilee's family, a school of dependents at his Canadian safehouse). The subject's response moves through the full escalation ladder catalogued in Section 5 and breaches it: he enters a prolonged berserker-adjacent state of *deliberate, sustained, cold violence* that is — and this is the new datum — *not amnestic*. He remembers what he does. He chooses it. The dissociative split is being replaced, in this arc, by an *integrated* lethal mode. Clinically this is ambiguous: integration is the goal of treatment, but the integrated content here is the violence, not the inhibition. He is, in effect, becoming able to do consciously what he used to require dissociation to do — which is a different problem, not a solution.

---

## F. Fall of X, the Orchis campaign, and Krakoa's collapse (2023–2024)

Orchis attacks the Hellfire Gala. The Resurrection Protocols are compromised. Krakoa as a sovereign mutant home is destroyed. The subject is separated from the Council, from the Summer House configuration, from the Green Lagoon, from X-Force's institutional cover, and from the resurrection safety net — *all the exoskeletal supports for the disorder are removed at once.*

His Fall-of-X-era behavior reverts to the most classical version of himself observable in the file: solo, geographically displaced, predator-mode, no institution. He hunts Orchis cells. He resurfaces in border towns. The cigar/alcohol/wilderness configuration of the early Claremont era recurs almost beat-for-beat. The diagnostic point is that under sustained institutional stress *his behavior regresses to the earliest stable equilibrium he ever achieved* — which is the lone, traveling, vengeance-and-mercy operator of *Wolverine* vol. 2 in the late 1980s. The default settings reassert under load.

Specific late-Fall-of-X data points:

- He carries personal effects again — a small pack rather than a Krakoan-portal pocket. The reversion to physical-object dependence is itself notable for a man who had grown accustomed to Krakoan logistics.
- He sleeps in vehicles, in motels under aliases that recycle the **"Patch"** Madripoor-era handle and variants. Aliases-of-prior-eras under stress: an identity-conservation behavior consistent with the Şar identity-alteration spectrum — he reaches for prior selves as templates when the present one is unsustainable.
- His olfactory hypervigilance is observed to be running at saturation; he reports — in dialogue, *Wolverine* vol. 7 late issues — being able to smell Orchis biotech at distance. The sensory-burden problem (Section 2) is *adaptive* in active hunt-mode, which is part of why hunt-mode is his most regulated state. The disorder is congruent with the task.

---

## G. *From the Ashes* and present configuration (2024–present)

In the *From the Ashes* relaunch, the mutant diaspora reorganizes into smaller cells. The subject is operating, at the time of this dossier, primarily out of a remote location (the *Wolverine* vol. 8 ongoing, Kelly Thompson, places him in Alaska / the North; the parallel *Weapon X-Men* and crossover appearances place him intermittently in X-Force-adjacent ops). The Alaska basing is, structurally, a return to the Yukon mining-camp exile of the *Origin* aftermath — *the first stable post-trauma equilibrium of his life was a sub-Arctic isolation*, and at every subsequent major decompensation he returns to a topographic and climatic analog of it. This is the most consistent geographic finding in the file. **Cold, low-population, high-wilderness north** is his self-prescribed convalescent setting; he has used it after the Howlett incident, after Weapon X, after Mariko's death, after the original Wolverine miniseries fallout, after *Old Man Logan*-continuity displacement, and now after Krakoa.

Current behavioral state (synthesis of latest available canon):

- **Memory:** intact for recent events; the chronic substrate of pre-Weapon-X uncertainty persists and is, at this point, *accepted* rather than actively investigated. He has stopped chasing his origin. This is either resolution or exhaustion; the file cannot distinguish.
- **Affect:** flatter than the school-era baseline. The Krakoan losses have not been mourned in any observable ritual; he is in the avoidance-phase of grief, expressed as work.
- **Relationships:** Laura is the primary live attachment; Jubilee, Kitty (now Kate Pryde), and Kurt are in contact but geographically remote. Jean is — depending on which thread is current — alive but post-Krakoan, and the Summer House configuration is functionally suspended. Daken is in his own orbit. Sabretooth is, again, alive and in the world: the chronic destabilizer is restored to its long-run baseline.
- **Substance use:** continued, at maintenance dose. No observed escalation, no observed reduction.
- **Violence:** integrated/conscious mode (per *Sabretooth War*) persists; berserker dissociation appears less frequent in current issues, which I read as *the integration of the violent self into the conscious self.* This is, again, ambiguous gain. The container is holding because its walls have moved inward.
- **Mentorship:** continues. Where there are young mutants in the post-Krakoan diaspora needing protection, he is among them. The drive has outlasted every institution that ever housed it.
- **Self-narration:** he speaks less. The verbal sardonicism of the Claremont and Aaron eras is reduced. In interview-format scenes (the rare ones in current runs) he answers in short factual statements. This is consistent with late-stage CPTSD presentation in long-survivor populations: the narrative apparatus is conserved for action, not exposition.

---

## H. How he got here — the throughline

The path from the Schism (school-as-vocation) → death (literalized adamantium burial) → return (re-implanted, again) → Krakoa (disorder externalized as institution) → Fall (institution removed, baseline reasserts) → present (cold north, small attachments, integrated violence, accepted amnesia) is — when laid against the longitudinal record in Section 1 — *the same arc he has run several times before, at smaller scale.* Each cycle: he accepts an institutional container; the container fails or is taken; he returns to wilderness; he rebuilds smaller. The amplitude of the cycle is not decreasing, but the *recovery time* between collapse and re-engagement *is.* He is, at 130+ years of life and after the most recent institutional catastrophe of his career, *back in the field within months* rather than within years. This is the measurable index of late-life compensatory consolidation: not that the disorder is smaller, but that the recovery scaffolding is faster to deploy because he has built it so many times.

## I. Current operational status (file summary)

- **Location:** sub-Arctic North America, mobile, no fixed institutional address.
- **Affiliations:** loose X-Men diaspora; X-Force-adjacent black ops as called; no Council, no school headship, no Avengers slot.
- **Health:** healing factor nominal; adamantium load chronic; sensory baseline saturated.
- **Psychiatric:** CPTSD and dissociative-spectrum syndrome (per Şar 2014, 2022) — *clinically stable in the sense that the patient has built workable, if costly, compensations,* not in the sense of remission. The compensations are: cold-north geography, alcohol-at-dose, mentorship as vocational anchor, integrated rather than dissociated violence, small attachments rather than institutional ones.
- **Risk profile (to self):** chronic, low-grade, lifelong; not acute. He will continue to put himself in lethal situations and will continue to be hard to kill. The wish-for-an-ending noted in Section 5 is present but not acute.
- **Risk profile (to others):** controlled. He has, in this most recent era, refined the conscious-violence mode such that civilian collateral is observably lower than in prior decades. The integration's one virtue.
- **Likely next-cycle trigger:** harm to Laura, Jubilee, or any minor under his current protection; or surfacing of a new agent claiming "your memories aren't yours." Both will produce the documented escalation sequence; both have been used before; both will be used again.

The file remains open. The subject is, at present, *as well as he has ever been,* which is a sentence that requires the entire preceding dossier to read correctly.


## Medical History

# MEDICAL HISTORY — SUBJECT: LOGAN

*File section M. Cross-reference with Section 3 (Psychological) and Section 4 (Psychiatric). Chronological wherever the canon permits; thematic where chronology is corrupted by amnestic gaps or implanted-memory overlays.*

---

## M.1 Constitutional Baseline and Genetic Endowment

The subject's somatic baseline is anomalous in three distinct registers, each of which has independent medical consequences and each of which carries its own psychological freight.

**Mutant phenotype, expressed (X-gene activation, peripubertal onset ca. 1897, Alberta).** The defining genetic endowment manifests in four linked traits: (i) accelerated tissue regeneration ("healing factor"), with documented capacity to reconstitute soft tissue within seconds, bone within hours, and — under sufficient cellular substrate — entire body mass from cardiac remnants (*Wolverine* vol. 3 #57, the Lazaer arc); (ii) negligible biological senescence past somatic maturity, producing a phenotypic age fixed in the apparent fifth decade across a chronological lifespan now exceeding 130 years; (iii) hyperacute sensoria across olfactory, auditory, and visual modalities, with documented capacity to track scent at distances and ages no canine olfactory bulb can match, to discriminate elevated heart rate and skin-conductance changes (i.e., to *smell a lie*), and to register the metabolic signatures of fear, arousal, illness, intoxication, and ovulation in proximate humans; (iv) three pairs of triple osseous claws — two dorsal-manual, one dorsal-pedal in some depictions — extruding from intra-osseous housings in the radius/ulna complex.

**Pre-mutation phenotype (childhood, late 1880s–early 1890s, Howlett estate).** A *sickly* child. Documented asthma or asthma-analog respiratory fragility, frequent confinement, pallor, undersized stature relative to peers. The medical irony is structural: the man who becomes the most physiologically durable being in his cohort began as the frailest child in his own household. This pre-mutation invalid identity is psychologically load-bearing — the *animal* self-concept (Section 3) is in part a counter-formation against the *sickly little boy* he was first told he was.

**Iatrogenic skeletal modification — adamantium graft.** Discussed in extenso at M.5. Note here only that his current somatic baseline cannot be assessed without it: every measurement post-1960s/70s (canonical dating fluid) is the measurement of a body with approximately 100 lb of foreign metal molecularly fused to its osseous matrix.

---

## M.2 Childhood and Adolescent Medical Record (1880s–ca. 1900)

**Constitutional fragility.** Per *Origin* #1–6: respiratory delicacy sufficient to keep him indoors; tutored privately rather than schooled; described by household staff in terms reserved for invalids. No documented chronic infection but recurrent acute presentations consistent with reactive airway disease. Skin sensitivity and photophobia hinted at — he is depicted preferring interior dimness.

**Index trauma and first claw extrusion (Howlett estate, night of the John Howlett killing).** The acute presentation is unambiguous: catastrophic adrenergic surge in response to witnessed parricide → first transcutaneous extrusion of six bone claws through previously intact dorsal-manual fascia and dermis. The procedure is, in soft-tissue terms, a bilateral compound laceration self-inflicted from within. Bleeding is documented. Healing factor at this point is undocumented but inferable (no infection, rapid closure). Psychological encoding is total and indelible: *the act of self-defense IS self-wounding*; he cannot protect without bleeding. This equation is never undone.

**Killing of Thomas Logan (biological father, not yet known as such).** First kill. Soft-tissue contact with claws-in-living-flesh — sensory data which the hyperacute nervous system will store with photographic precision and which will recur as intrusive imagery for the next century.

**Accidental killing of Rose by claw impalement (Yukon mining camp, ca. 1897).** During fight with Dog/Thomas Logan's son. The first instance of the canonical *beloved dies on the claws* pattern. Medically: penetrating thoracic trauma, exsanguination, death within minutes. Psychologically: the claws are now permanently coded as instruments of intimate harm, not only of defense. From this point forward, every claw extrusion in proximity to an attachment figure carries a *contraindication* he cannot articulate but acts on.

**Feral interval (Yukon wilderness, late 1890s).** Years of unsheltered subarctic exposure with wolf-pack integration. Medically remarkable for what it implies about the healing factor and thermoregulation: he survived. Nutritional state likely carnivorous-near-exclusive, with implications for the later olfactory/gustatory preference profile (the subject's lifelong preference for rare red meat and his physiological under-response to gastrointestinal pathogens both trace plausibly here). Dental record: incisor wear patterns consistent with raw-bone work.

---

## M.3 Early Twentieth Century — Combat Acquisition Period (ca. 1900–1939)

**Cumulative penetrating and blunt trauma, undocumented but inferable.** Spanish-American adjacent conflicts, WWI trench service, interwar mercenary work, Spanish Civil War. The healing factor is by this point well-established and presumably fully tuned: subject is functionally immune to bacterial wound infection, gas exposure (mustard, chlorine), and the chronic respiratory sequelae that disabled most of his contemporaries.

**Substance acquisition.** Tobacco use begins in this period, almost certainly in trench/camp context. Cigar preference (over cigarette) likely consolidates in the 1920s–30s; the choice is medically incidental but behaviorally diagnostic — it is a *ritualized*, slow, deliberate intake rather than a continuous nicotine drip. Ethanol use is presumed continuous from age of access onward, with no documented period of abstinence longer than the Bushidō training intervals at Jasmine Falls.

**Jasmine Falls integration (Japan, pre-WWII, exact dates obscured by retcons).** First period of relative somatic regulation in the record. Bushidō training under Bandō Saburō imposes diurnal structure, fasting, controlled breathing, kata, meditation. This is the only documented period in which alcohol use *decreases* by behavioral inference. The Itsu relationship and her subsequent murder while pregnant (Daken, *Wolverine: Origins*) terminate it. Penetrating abdominal trauma to Itsu (Winter Soldier per retcon) — Daken extracted post-mortem in utero. Subject's somatic response to her loss is not directly documented but the subsequent decade is the most dissociated and behaviorally dysregulated of the pre-Weapon X record.

---

## M.4 WWII through Team X (ca. 1939–1968, dating soft)

**Combat injury accrual** at a rate that for any non-mutant would constitute serial fatalities. The medical fact of interest is the *training effect on pain tolerance and parasuicidal recklessness*. Across this period he learns — and is conditioned by repetition — that no wound is terminal. This is the substrate of the lifelong behavioral marker: *he uses his own body as a tactical resource* (charging gunfire, taking the blade to close range, jumping from altitude). In any non-mutant this would warrant a parasuicidal-behavior diagnosis. In him it is reality-tested and reinforced.

**Team X medical record.** Documented (*Wolverine* vol. 2 #48–50, "Logan: A Dog's Life") implantation of false memories beginning in this period — not yet the adamantium procedure, but neurological/pharmacological manipulation under CIA/black-ops auspices. The first documented *iatrogenic identity injury*: he leaves Team X with autobiographical content he will spend the rest of his life unable to verify. Concurrent psychotropic exposure presumed (the implantation methods canonically involve drug-assisted hypnosis).

**Adversarial pair-bond with Sabretooth, soft-tissue record.** Annual "birthday" attempts, century-spanning. The accumulated mutual-laceration history between Logan and Creed is, in a literal medical sense, the largest single dataset of healing-factor-on-healing-factor combat trauma in existence. He has had his throat opened by Creed more than once; the scar tissue does not persist, but the *anticipatory autonomic response to Creed's specific scent signature* is now hard-wired at brainstem level.

---

## M.5 Weapon X (Windsor-Smith, *Marvel Comics Presents* #72–84) — the defining iatrogenic injury

The single most consequential medical event in the file. Reconstruction:

**Abduction and induction.** Subject taken in unknown circumstances (memory corrupted). Confined in surgical-grade restraint apparatus. Stripped, shaved, catheterized, electrode-instrumented. The induction protocol is *deliberately depersonalizing*: he is addressed as "the animal," numbered, denied verbal interaction, kept in cold and dim conditions, fed through tubes. This is not incidental — it is the engineered prerequisite for the dissociative encoding that follows.

**Adamantium bonding procedure.** Molecular-level infusion of liquefied adamantium into the entire osseous matrix, including the existing osseous claws (now adamantium-sheathed). The procedure is performed while the subject is paralytically immobilized but, per the record, *not fully anesthetized for all portions* — he is conscious for parts of the bonding. Pain load: unimaginable to any reference patient. The healing factor's role is grotesque: it permits the procedure to occur at all by preventing death from cardiovascular shock, while simultaneously *prolonging* the conscious experience of it. He cannot die out of it. The graft does not fail; the body adapts.

**Permanent sequelae of the graft:**
- *Chronic heavy-metal toxicity load,* continuously buffered by the healing factor. When the factor is suppressed (mechanical/psionic/pharmacological), toxicity rapidly degrades hepatic, renal, and neurological function — documented in *Death of Wolverine* (2014), where loss of factor + adamantium load produces lethal physiological collapse over weeks.
- *Mass loading* of approximately 100 lb above somatic baseline, with corresponding cardiovascular workload, joint stress, and buoyancy negative — he sinks. This is non-trivial: terminal drowning in liquid adamantium (*Death of Wolverine*) is, somatically, the inversion of the inducing procedure.
- *Claw extrusion now lacerates dorsal hand tissue against adamantium-sheathed bone every time.* Every defensive act produces bilateral hand wounds that heal within seconds but *do bleed and do hurt*. Pain is the prerequisite of his primary defensive behavior. This is the most under-discussed medical fact in the file and the most psychologically consequential: he cannot defend himself or anyone else without immediate self-injury. The Rose equation, encoded somatically, reinforced thousands of times.
- *Concurrent psychosurgical/conditioning programming* — kill-command implants, handler-recognition cues, behavioral overrides. Functionally a chemically-and-conditioning-induced acute dissociative state engineered on demand. He escapes in a berserker fugue, kills the surgical and command staff, and is recovered naked, hypothermic, and amnestic in the snow by James and Heather Hudson.

**Aftermath presentation, Hudson recovery.** Hypothermia, malnutrition, dehydration, complete autobiographical amnesia, behaviorally regressed to feral state. The Hudsons provide the first post-trauma holding environment; this period is the proximate origin of his capacity for trustable adult attachment, and the reason "James" (Hudson) is a load-bearing name for him for decades after.

---

## M.6 Post-Weapon X Injury Catalogue (selected; the comprehensive list is impractical)

A non-exhaustive enumeration of injuries the subject has *sustained and survived*, with notes on the medical and psychological residue of each. The pattern across this catalogue is not the injuries themselves but the *cumulative conditioning effect*: each survival further entrenches the parasuicidal tactical style and the conviction that no ending will be permitted him.

- **Gunshot wounds, multi-caliber, multi-anatomic-region, hundreds of documented instances.** Healing factor closes soft-tissue tracks within minutes; bullet expulsion is sometimes manual, sometimes pushed out by tissue regeneration. No retained foreign bodies of medical significance.
- **Penetrating blade trauma, including katana through torso, claws of Sabretooth and Daken through abdomen and thorax, repeated.** No residual scar tissue. Autonomic anticipatory response to *specific* attackers (Creed scent signature, Hand metallurgical signature) is conditioned and persistent.
- **Immolation, multiple events.** Full-body burns to the point of muscular char (*Wolverine* vol. 2, Phoenix-adjacent arcs; *Enemy of the State*). Healing factor reconstitutes from cardiopulmonary core outward. The somatic memory of burn pain is encoded and produces a documentable fire-aversion in calm states that disappears in combat.
- **Decapitation-adjacent and skeletal extraction trauma.** *X-Men* #25 (Fatal Attractions): magnetic extraction of adamantium through every pore of the integument. Soft-tissue trauma comparable to inverse vivisection. Recovery prolonged; identity-stabilizing effects of the *removal* of adamantium are noted in the file as paradoxical — without the metal he becomes more feral, the bone claws re-emerge, and Genesis subsequently attempts re-bonding (*Wolverine* vol. 2 #100), which his body rejects in a brief window before re-acceptance.
- **Vivisection by Apocalypse (*Wolverine* vol. 2 #145).** Forcible separation of left arm and somatic violation under control conditioning; conversion into the Horseman Death. This is the *second* major iatrogenic identity-overwrite (after Weapon X), with comparable psychological severity.
- **Drowning in liquefied adamantium (*Death of Wolverine*, 2014).** Subject's healing factor having been previously suppressed by infection-vector pathogens engineered by Cornelius's successors, terminal encasement in cooling adamantium. Cause of death: asphyxiation within a body that could no longer reconstruct itself. The symbolic completion of the Weapon X procedure: the metal that lined his bones now lines the exterior of his body. He is buried in his own armor.
- **Post-resurrection presentation (*Return of Wolverine*, 2018).** Healing factor restored, memory fragmented anew, Persephone-implanted kill triggers active. The cycle is now demonstrably *structural*: even death does not exit it.
- **Krakoan resurrection-protocol cycle (2019+).** The death/restoration sequence becomes institutional. Behaviorally significant: subject undergoes deaths in the Krakoan era at a rate that, even granting institutional context, indicates a normalized parasuicidal operating tempo.

---

## M.7 Substance Use — Detailed Profile

**Ethanol.** Sustained heavy daily use across the entire documented adult lifespan. Preferred preparations: beer (volume), whisky and rye (efficacy), local spirits as available. The healing factor metabolizes ethanol at a rate orders of magnitude above normative human hepatic clearance, requiring intake sufficient that *the act of drinking is the goal as much as intoxication*. Behaviorally: the ritual of the bar — the slow nurse of a glass, the cigar, the back-to-the-wall seat with sightlines on the door — is itself the anxiolytic. He achieves brief, partial intoxication only with specific preparations engineered for mutant metabolism (Asgardian mead documented; certain Madripoor-distilled liquors functionally effective). The psychological function is unambiguous: pharmacological compensation for absent endogenous affect regulation. Functional Alcohol Use Disorder by behavioral criteria (Section 4).

**Tobacco (cigars predominant; occasional cigarettes).** Continuous use, century-plus duration. No pulmonary sequelae (healing factor). Psychological function: ritualized self-regulation, oral fixation, occupied hands, sensory dampening of his own hyperacute olfaction in environments where the ambient scent load is intolerable. The cigar is also a *temporal* tool — it imposes a 30-to-60-minute period during which he is committed to stillness. This is one of his few self-prescribed regulating behaviors.

**Caffeine (coffee predominant).** Heavy use, ineffective stimulant action, ritual function only.

**Psychotropics, involuntary (extensive).** Weapon X induction agents; Team X memory-implantation pharmacology; Hand hypnotics; Mojoverse compliance drugs; Persephone resurrection conditioning agents; assorted villain-of-the-week chemistries. The cumulative pharmacological insult to the central nervous system is incalculable. The healing factor clears agents rapidly but does *not* reverse conditioning effects once established — the agents are vehicles for behavioral programming that persists in the absence of the agent.

**Psychotropics, voluntary (psychiatric).** Effectively nil. He does not engage with psychiatric medication. Tolerance and metabolism would render most agents subtherapeutic without dosing protocols that no responsible clinician would attempt; in addition, the subject's authority-distrust and his unwillingness to permit chemical entry into a CNS that has been weaponized against him repeatedly preclude compliance.

**Recreational drugs.** Largely absent. The same metabolism-and-trust profile applies. He has been forcibly dosed; he does not self-administer.

---

## M.8 Sensory Burden as Medical Condition

The hyperacute sensoria are not unalloyed gifts and warrant medical-record framing.

**Olfaction.** Continuous involuntary intake of: human fear pheromones (skin volatiles, axillary secretions, breath ketones of stress); arousal markers; illness markers (the metabolic signature of certain cancers, diabetic ketoacidosis, hepatic failure — he can *smell* terminal illness in proximate persons); deception markers (sympathetic skin conductance, cortisol pulse, micro-changes in respiratory rate detectable via exhaled-air composition); reproductive-cycle markers in proximate women. The clinical consequence: he cannot occupy normal social space without involuntary intimate knowledge of every occupant. The behavioral consequences are pervasive — choice of seating, choice of cities, choice of solitude, ventilation behaviors, the cigar as olfactory occluder.

**Audition.** Conversation at sotto voce across rooms; vascular pulse of proximate persons; mechanical signatures of weapons and engines. Imposes continuous auditory triage in any populated environment.

**Vision.** Documented low-light acuity; motion-detection at the threshold of avian raptors.

**Net effect.** Anatomical hypervigilance. The DSM hypervigilance criterion for PTSD is, in him, partially *anatomically imposed* and cannot be extinguished by therapy. This is medically important: standard trauma-treatment protocols predicated on extinction of conditioned hypervigilance will partially fail in this patient because the sensory substrate keeps re-presenting the cues.

---

## M.9 Reproductive and Familial Medical Record

Confirmed biological offspring: Daken (Akihiro), conceived with Itsu, extracted in utero post-mortem. X-23 (Laura Kinney) is a somatic-cell-derived genetic derivative, not biological offspring in the conventional sense; the Stepford Cuckoos and various other genetic-derivative entities exist in the periphery. No documented stable pair-bonded reproductive history. Sexual transience across the century is well-documented and is best read as an avoidance correlate of the Rose/Itsu/Mariko template (Section 3) — the prediction that intimate partners will die because of him is a load-bearing belief and serial transience is its behavioral discharge.

---

## M.10 Disability Profile

The subject presents no *physical* disability in conventional terms; he is the inverse case. He presents profound *psychiatric and cognitive disability* (Section 4) that the healing factor cannot touch and that is in important respects *produced by* the same physiology that protects him from physical disability: the lack of permanent physical consequences has trained a tactical recklessness that has, in turn, multiplied his trauma exposure beyond what any conventional body could have accrued.

Specific functional impairments of note:
- *Autobiographical memory unreliability* sufficient to constitute a chronic cognitive disability. He cannot verify his own past. He treats memory as evidence to be cross-examined rather than as identity. Adaptive but disabling.
- *Affect-regulation failure* at the high-arousal end, with acute dissociative episodes (berserker state) constituting a periodic loss of behavioral control and post-episodic amnesia.
- *Interpersonal-intimacy impairment* — the approach-withdrawal cycle (Section 3).
- *Diurnal-regulation impairment* — disordered sleep, nightmares (the intrusive-memory criterion of CPTSD), early waking, frequent geographic re-location.

---

## M.11 Per-Event Psychological Impact — Summary Table in Prose

The first claw extrusion encoded *self-defense = self-wounding*. Rose's death on his claws encoded *love-object dies by my instrument*. The Howlett night encoded *the category of father collapses* (Section 3). Itsu's murder repeated and deepened the Rose template and added *I cannot protect a pregnant woman in my house*. Weapon X encoded *my body is not mine; my memory is not mine; my will is not mine* — the etiological signature for the dissociative spectrum disorder per Şar (2014, 2022) — and added the permanent somatic equation *every defensive act bleeds my hands*. Team X added *people I trusted as comrades were also handlers*. Mariko's death by his hand at her request encoded *even mercy from me looks like the same act* — and consolidated the belief that he is unfit for the samurai role he most wants. Magneto's extraction of the adamantium encoded *the violation is also revisitable from the outside whenever sufficient force is applied*. Apocalypse's Death conversion repeated Weapon X at the level of identity overwrite, demonstrating that no defensive structure he had built was adequate. *Enemy of the State* (Hand/Hydra programming) demonstrated the same point at the level of behavior — his body could be turned against his comrades again, by a different operator, with the same result. *Old Man Logan* (Mysterio overlay leading to slaughter of the X-Men) is the inverse: the dissociative weapon-self contaminated the autobiographical self so thoro


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — SUBJECT: LOGAN

*Compiled from longitudinal observation across the published record, 1974–present; cross-checked across artists (Cockrum, Byrne, Miller, Buscema, Silvestri, Kubert, Madureira, Quesada, Jae Lee, Romita Jr., McNiven, Larroca, Yu), whose convergent visual record on certain micro-behaviors is itself evidentiary. Where artists diverge, behavior cited has appeared in at least three independent runs.*

---

## I. ANTHROPOMETRY & STANDING FORM

Stature is short — canonically 5'3" pre-adamantium, 5'3"–5'5" depending on artist's discipline; mass approximately 195 lb naked, 300+ lb skeletally bonded (the adamantium load is visible in his footprint depth in soft ground, in the way wooden floors creak under him, in the way mattresses compress). The body is small, dense, and disproportionate: brachycephalic skull, short thick neck obscured by trapezius hypertrophy, deltoid-to-waist ratio extreme, forearms grotesquely overdeveloped relative to upper arms (a century of three-times-daily claw extrusion against bone load is a unique resistance regimen — the brachioradialis and flexor mass are the body's signature). Carriage low and forward: center of gravity at navel rather than chest, knees never quite locked, weight habitually on the balls of the feet. He occupies less vertical space than he could; the trapezius is rolled slightly forward, head dropped between the shoulders. This is the wolverine carriage of a man who has spent decades expecting to be hit from above and behind.

**Posture by state.** *Calm:* slouched, weight on one hip, often leaning — wall, doorframe, bar rail, tree. He does not stand free in open space if a vertical surface is available; the back wants cover. *Social/teaching:* posture squares minimally, hands often in pockets or folded across chest, chin tucks. *Stress/threat-assessment:* the slouch tightens into a coiled half-crouch, knees deepen a quarter-inch, the trapezius rises perceptibly, head drops further, shoulders rotate forward to protect the throat. *Combat-engaged:* the body breaks into a low, wide quadrupedal stance, weight distributed almost evenly between feet, slightly anterior; arms held away from the trunk to clear the forearm extrusion path. *Berserker-dissociated:* posture inverts. Slouch abandoned. Spine extends fully, head thrown back, chest opens, mouth opens — a brief vertical *display* before the four-limbed lunge. Artists from Miller forward render this consistently and it is the single clearest exterior marker of state shift.

---

## II. GAIT, LOCOMOTION, AND OCCUPATION OF SPACE

Gait is short-stride, heavy-heeled, deliberate. Cadence approximately 100 steps/min at ambulation, with notable foot-fall asymmetry: the right side strikes marginally harder (long-standing favored claw-arm; the body has rebalanced around the right-forearm load). Toes engage late; the push-off is from midfoot rather than forefoot — a *tracker's* gait, low and quiet on natural surfaces, surprisingly loud on hardwood because of mass. On soft ground he goes near-silent and shifts to a heel-light, outer-edge-of-foot placement learned in the Yukon period and reinforced in Japan.

**Spatial occupation patterns.** Enters rooms along the wall, never down the centerline. Locates exits within the first three seconds — the eyes do a brief sweep, ceiling first (vents, skylights), then door, then window, then occupants. Selects seating with back to wall and line of sight to entry; will displace others to obtain this without comment. In booths, takes the seat facing the door. On airplanes, aisle seat at the rear. In elevators, back corner, facing the doors, weight on rear foot. Will not stand under hanging fixtures by preference. Refuses to walk through revolving doors at normal speed and will wait for a clear quadrant. None of this is verbalized; observed only by what he *does not* do.

**Stairs:** descends with hand off the rail and slight forward lean, takes two at a time when alone. **Doorways:** pauses a half-beat at the threshold of an unfamiliar room — a nasal sample, not visual. **Outdoors:** circles a campsite once before settling. **Indoors at night:** the route from bed to door is rehearsed; he walks it once on first occupying a room.

---

## III. THE FACE — RESTING, EXPRESSIVE, AND TELL-PATTERN

The face is broad, prognathic, with heavy supraorbital ridges that throw the eyes into permanent shadow — an anatomic asset for a man whose work depends on others not reading him. Resting expression is a flat-affect downturn: corners of the mouth at neutral or below, masseter slightly engaged (chronic clench — bruxism is presumed; the healing factor erases dental evidence). The eyes track without head movement, a saccadic style that reads as predatory.

**Hair.** The mutton-chop sideburns are immutable across all eras and identities — Patch, Death, Old Man, Weapon X-era, Krakoan — they regenerate to a fixed pattern post-injury, suggesting either a follicular genetic determinism or (more interpretively) that the body's regeneration template was somatically *fixed* at a particular life-moment, possibly the Howlett-to-Logan transition. The double-peaked hair is similarly invariant; he does not style it and it does not move. Body hair is heavy on chest, forearms, lower legs; absent on the dorsal hands at the extrusion sites (chronic micro-scarring prevents regrowth there — the only place on his body where the healing factor leaves a permanent topographical mark).

**Facial micro-tells, by state.**
- *Lying or being lied to:* the right corner of the mouth ticks up a millimeter — a half-sneer he is unaware of. He smells the lie before he hears it; the tic precedes the verbal challenge by 200–400 ms.
- *Recognition of an enemy by scent:* nostrils flare, the jaw sets, breath holds for a beat, then exhales through the nose. He does not turn his head toward the source until after the exhale.
- *Suppressed grief:* a single hard blink, head tilts down two degrees, the jaw shifts laterally once. He does not water-tear in public; the canon record of him weeping is short and almost exclusively in private or beside the dying (Mariko, Jean variants, Charles).
- *Genuine amusement:* a closed-mouth huff through the nose, shoulders move once. Open-mouth laughter is rare and almost always alcohol-disinhibited.
- *Dissociative onset:* the eyes lose convergent focus — they go *flat*, pupils dilate disproportionately to ambient light, the brow drops, the upper lip retracts to expose the upper canines. This is the moment to leave the room. Observers who have survived him at length (Kitty, Kurt, Ororo) read it and move; novice observers do not.
- *Post-episode reorientation:* the gaze ticks rapidly across the immediate environment, then down to his own hands. The hands check is invariant. He needs to see what they have done before he can resume identity.

**The chewing-cigar oral pattern.** The cigar is in the mouth during waking hours at perhaps 60% baseline; in stress it rises to 90%. He chews more than he smokes — the healing factor metabolizes tobacco fast enough that nicotine effect is marginal, suggesting the cigar's primary function is *oral occupation* and *olfactory baffle* (a strong nearby scent partially masks the hyperacute background). Rolls the cigar across his teeth left-to-right with the tongue when thinking; clamps it hard in the right molars when angry; removes it entirely before combat and pockets it (he does not drop or waste them). The cigar's position is a state-readable gauge.

---

## IV. THE HANDS — MOST OBSERVABLE INSTRUMENT

The hands are the most surveillance-relevant body region. Short, thick fingers, heavily callused along the ulnar edges and across the proximal phalanges; the dorsal surface bears a faint triple parallel scarring at the second-third-fourth metacarpal interspaces — the only chronic somatic record on him, the claw-extrusion sites where healing is asymptotically perfect but never quite resets. Faint blood often visible at these sites for 10–60 seconds post-retraction before resorption.

**Resting hand behavior.** Hands rarely still. Idle behaviors: drumming the right index finger against thigh or table at approximately 2 Hz; thumbing the lip of a glass; rolling a coin, lighter, or knife handle through the fingers (a manual rehearsal that may serve to keep the fine motor distinct from the gross-motor claw reflex). When seated and unoccupied, the right hand will often rest palm-down with fingers slightly curled — the extrusion-ready position — on the thigh; the left rests open. This handedness asymmetry is consistent across artists.

**Claw extrusion behavior.** The extrusion itself is a rapid pronation-fist-and-thrust, the wrist locks, the dorsal skin parts at the three established channels. The accompanying *snikt* is the most documented vocalization in the file but is mechanical, not phonatory. Extrusion as warning is single-claw (the middle): a slow, controlled extension, often without looking at the hand — eye contact maintained with the target. Two-claw extension is rare and usually a tactical signal to teammates. Full three-claw extension is committed combat or display. He has been observed to extrude one claw absently while thinking — at a kitchen table, in conversation with Xavier, in moments of decision pressure. He notices, retracts, apologizes (or does not).

**Grooming and hand hygiene.** He washes the hands compulsively after combat — not for sanitation (the healing factor handles infection) but for the blood, which his own olfactory load makes intolerable on his person. Will use snow, river water, vodka, anything to hand. Does not bite nails (the healing factor outpaces growth at the bed; nails are constant length). Does not wear rings, watches, or bracelets — anything on the wrists interferes with extrusion clearance.

---

## V. GROOMING, DRESS, AND BODILY MAINTENANCE

Shaving is unnecessary at the sideburns/scalp (template-fixed) but performed at the cheeks and throat — daily, with a straight razor by preference, learned in the Yukon period and continued ritually. The straight razor is itself a tell: a man who handles a blade at his own throat daily is rehearsing his relationship to mortality. He does it without a mirror as readily as with one.

Dress is utilitarian and consistent across eras when out of uniform: denim, flannel, leather, boots with a defined heel for stirrup-and-stride purchase, belt with a heavy buckle (improvised weapon and weighted handhold). Layers always allow forearm clearance; he does not wear cuffed sleeves buttoned at the wrist by preference. Cold weather: he under-dresses systematically (the metabolic load of the healing factor produces a base body temperature 1–2°F above human normal; he runs hot). Footwear is worn until destroyed; he does not replace serviceable boots for fashion. Owns very little. Possessions cluster around: blades (knives in varied carry positions, ritually maintained), one or two articles of clothing per environment, a small set of personal-history objects (Mariko's photograph at various times, Silver Fox totems, items from Jean) — these latter rotate in and out of his possession across decades, sometimes lost in fugue periods and reacquired.

Bathing pattern: showers cold by preference (thermal regulation; possibly also dissociation-management — cold water is a classic acute-dissociation grounding tool, and his body learned this empirically before psychiatry named it). Long submersion in hot baths only in Japan, and only ritually — onsen and ofuro as part of the Bushidō container. The two bathing modes correlate with his two operational selves.

---

## VI. EATING AND DRINKING

Caloric load is enormous — estimated 6,000–10,000 kcal/day baseline, multiples of that under regeneration demand. Eats fast, head low over the plate, fork in fist (continental grip ignored), free hand on the table edge. Will eat alone preferentially; in company, finishes well before others and pushes back from the table. Prefers high-protein, high-fat, simple foods: red meat (rare to the point of bloody), eggs, root vegetables, bread. Tolerates Japanese cuisine with respect — sashimi, rice, miso — and the etiquette markedly slows and formalizes him there (chopsticks held correctly, posture squared, pace matched to host). This is the cleanest behavioral demonstration that he *can* eat in a regulated way and chooses not to elsewhere.

**Alcohol.** Sustained, heavy, functionally constant. Beer as base load (Molson and similar Canadian lagers in the canonical record; six-to-twelve at a sitting without observable effect). Whiskey, bourbon, sake as targeted intake — drinks straight, neat, doubles, will down a shot without facial reaction. Has been depicted putting away a bottle of hard liquor across a long evening with only mild intoxication. Achieves intoxication only at extreme volume (multiple bottles or with healing-factor suppression). The drinking is paced and constant rather than binge-cyclical — a maintenance pour throughout the day. Functional read: chronic anxiolytic self-administration against a hyperarousal his physiology will not let him down from.

**Hydration and intake of plain water:** low. He is a chronic mild dehydrator; the healing factor compensates.

---

## VII. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

Sleeps lightly and in fragments. Total sleep time approximately 4–5 hours/24-hour cycle in normal operation, distributed in two or three blocks rather than one consolidated period — a polyphasic adaptation from the military century. Will not lie flat on his back voluntarily; sleeps on his side, often the right (claw arm) facing out from the wall, left ear to pillow (the dominant ear remains exposed to the room). Cover use minimal regardless of temperature. Sleeps clothed or partially clothed if not in a secured environment; fully unclothed only with trusted partners or alone in known terrain.

**Sleep environment.** Window cracked for olfactory access to the outside; door angle calculated; weapon (knife, in non-claw eras a sidearm) within reach. Has been observed to wake to a footstep at a hundred meters; wakes to a *change* in ambient scent (someone enters the building, a fire is lit, a familiar enemy comes within radius). Wake-to-action latency under 400 ms — he is upright with claws extended before the eyes finish opening, an autonomic startle that has injured well-meaning bedmates on more than one canonical occasion.

**Dreams and nightmares.** Documented across runs (Claremont's interior monologue passages, Aaron's *Astonishing Tales*, the *Origin* coda): nightmares are vivid and somatic — Weapon X imagery, Rose's death, the women on his claws. He thrashes; he has spoken in his sleep in three languages (English, Japanese, Cheyenne in older runs). Pre-sleep ritual when possible: alcohol, cigar, a short physical sequence (the Yashida kata at low intensity, or a perimeter walk). Does not nap socially; if he closes his eyes in company he is not asleep.

---

## VIII. RESPIRATION AND VOCAL PATTERN

Breathing at rest is slow and diaphragmatic, approximately 10–12 breaths/min; nasal inhalation by strong preference (the olfactory sampling is constant — he is *reading* the room with every breath). Mouth-breathing is a stress sign: shifts to mouth inhalation when a scent is overwhelming, when injured beyond the factor's instantaneous capacity, or when displaying aggression. In berserker state, breath becomes audible, low, growled on the exhale; this is the only routine vocalization in that state.

**Voice.** Baritone, gravelled (chronic alcohol and cigar use, healing-factor-stabilized), Albertan-Canadian substrate audible on certain vowels and on the *aboot*-class diphthongs across writers attentive to it. Speech is economical: short sentences, sentence fragments, Anglo-Saxon lexicon by preference. Honorifics appear in Japanese contexts with reflexive correctness ("-san," "-sensei," "-sama" used unprompted and appropriately). Profanity is constant, mild-to-moderate, used as punctuation rather than emphasis. Vocal pitch drops perceptibly under threat; rises slightly in genuine affection and around children. Whispering capacity is good — a tracker's tradecraft. Will go entirely silent under threat-assessment, sometimes for minutes; the silence itself is a state-marker.

**Idiolectic tics.** "Bub" (most documented address), "darlin'" (toward women in non-threat contexts), "kid" (toward anyone under sixty he protects), absence of his own first name in self-reference — he refers to himself as Logan, almost never as James or Jim. The avoidance is total enough to be diagnostic of the Howlett-self's foreclosure.

---

## IX. OLFACTION AS BEHAVIOR

The hyperacute olfaction is not a passive sense but a continuous behavior. Observable correlates: the half-second nasal pause at thresholds; the head tilt — chin up and toward the source — when sampling at distance; the subtle wrinkle of the nose at unpleasant scents (chemical, hospital, certain perfumes); the *avoidant* shift away from bleach, gun-cleaning solvent, formaldehyde (all Weapon X-associated). He can identify individuals at 50–100 m by scent and tracks emotional state (fear, arousal, illness, deception) on companions in real time. The interpersonal consequence is that *he knows things about people they have not said*, and the social rule he has imposed on himself is to not act on most of it — a constant suppression effort visible in the way he sometimes looks away from a person mid-conversation, blinks once, and reorients without comment.

Cologne, scented soap, fabric softener: avoided on his own person. He smells, faintly and to those of normal olfaction, of leather, tobacco, sweat, beer, and steel — a stable scent profile across decades.

---

## X. SEXUAL AND INTIMATE SOMATICS

Sexual history is long and serial, low on documented detail by canon convention but inferable in pattern. Partners are typically capable, hardened, often dangerous women within his operational world (Mystique, Domino, Yukio, Silver Fox, various) — intimacy with non-combatants is rare and ends badly. Approach behavior with a sexual partner: closer-than-normative proximity, deliberate eye contact, low voice, slow movement — a *predator-modulating-for-prey* deceleration that he is aware of and deploys consciously. Touch initiation is hand-to-face or hand-to-back-of-neck — controlling regions, soothing in intent but anatomically dominant.

Post-coital pattern: leaves the bed early; smokes; often departs the dwelling before morning. Does not cohabit easily. The exceptions (Mariko, briefly Jean in various continuities, Storm in some) are the relationships in which he most visibly *struggles* — sleep is poorer, alcohol intake higher, irritability up. Intimacy is somatically destabilizing for him in a way combat is not.

With non-sexual intimates (Kurt, Ororo, Kitty, Jubilee, Rogers, Laura): physical contact is sparing but specific. A hand on the shoulder, a brief one-armed shoulder-clasp embrace, the back of a hand to a young protégé's cheek. He does not initiate full frontal hugs; he receives them stiffly at first and then settles. With children and adolescents under his protection, he is touch-tolerant to a degree that surprises observers — Jubilee climbing on him, Kitty leaning against him, Laura wordlessly fitting under his arm. The protective-paternal mode is the only one in which he is somatically *open*.

---

## XI. PAIN, INJURY, AND SOMATIC SELF-REGARD

Pain response is suppressed but not absent. Takes wounds without facial reaction in front of others; in private, has been observed to grunt, swear, brace against walls during severe regeneration (limb regrowth, organ reconstitution). Does not flinch at needles, blades, ballistic strike preparation — anatomic habituation. *Does* flinch at restraint: any binding of the wrists, any approach with surgical equipment, any sound of a powered medical apparatus produces an immediate dissociative-spike risk. Hospitals are aversive; he will leave AMA from any inpatient setting within hours and treats medical staff with a wariness reserved otherwise for enemy combatants. This is the Weapon X conditioning — the most reliable behavioral trigger in his profile.

Self-inspection of injury is fast and matter-of-fact: looks, assesses, returns to task. Does not display wounds for sympathy and does not conceal them for pride; treats his body as equipment. Will, in private, run a fingertip along a freshly closed wound — the same gesture, observed across decades — a tactile verification that the body has done its job. This is the closest he comes to a self-soothing somatic ritual.

---

## XII. STATE-SHIFT SUMMARY (THE SURVEILLANCE READ)

A field observer reading him in real time tracks, in priority order: **cigar position** (mouth/hand/pocketed = ascending threat-readiness); **right-hand resting curl** (open/half-curled/fisted); **trapezius set** (down/level/raised); **nostril activity** (passive/flaring/held); **eye convergence** (focused/flat); **breath audibility** (silent/audible/growled); **verbal output** (laconic/sardonic/silent/growled). The progression from social baseline to berserker dissociation runs through these channels in roughly that sequence and can be read by a trained observer with 5–15 seconds of lead time before the claws clear the skin.

The reverse progression — from berserker back to baseline — is slower and goes through different channels: hand-check first (looking at what he has done), then breath regulation, then a physical withdrawal from the scene, then alcohol, then sleep or geographic flight. The post-episode somatics are the period of maximum *psychological* accessibility — he is, briefly, present to himself in a way the rest of his architecture is built to prevent. The protocols of any handler, friend, or institutional ally who wishes to work with him *over time* converge on the same operational fact: the body tells the truth he is not yet able to say, and it tells it about ninety seconds before the mouth catches up.


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

## 1. The Origin Template — How the Category "Bond" Was Built Wrong

The attachment system of the subject was assembled, and then shattered, on a single afternoon in Alberta in the late 1880s. To map the rest of the file one must hold this scene precisely in view, because every later relationship is a variation on the chord it struck.

Pre-incident, the child James Howlett presents with a textbook *insecure-anxious* pattern: sickly, asthmatic, kept indoors, emotionally over-attached to a non-parental caregiver (the servant girl Rose) because the actual parents — Elizabeth Howlett (depressive, institutionally absent) and John Howlett (formally affectionate, structurally remote) — do not function as a secure base. The household's emotional warmth is *outsourced* to the servant class. This is the first relational rule he learns: *love comes from below your station, never from where it ought to.* He will repeat it for a hundred and thirty years — every durable bond he forms will be with a subordinate, a student, an outcast, or a fellow asset, almost never with a peer of equivalent status, and *never* with an institutional parent.

Then the scene in *Origin* #2: Thomas Logan kills John Howlett in front of the boy. The bone claws extrude. The child kills his biological father (whom he believes to be only the groundskeeper) with the body of the man who raised him still in the room. In a single instant the category "father" is shown to be (a) lethal to know, (b) doubled and incoherent, (c) something the child himself destroys with his own body. Rose — the only intact love object remaining — leads him into exile, and within years he kills her too, accidentally, with the same claws. The template now reads: *the people I love die on my body, by my body, because of my body.* This is not a metaphor he carries. It is a load-bearing predictive belief that determines, ever after, whom he allows close and how he behaves when they get there.

By the framework of Main & Solomon, this is *disorganized attachment* in its purest form: the caregiver is simultaneously the source of safety and the source of terror, and the child's own body is the instrument of the harm. Disorganized attachment in adults produces exactly what the canon documents: approach-and-flee oscillation, dissociative episodes triggered by intimacy itself, and a stable preference for ritualized hostile relationships over uncertain warm ones. Read forward from Alberta, every later pattern is legible.

## 2. The Repeating Template — One Story, Many Names

Across six decades of published record, a single relational sequence recurs with the regularity of a metronome. It runs:

1. **Distance** — he refuses the bond. Sardonic deflection, "I work alone," geographic flight, the cigar held between him and the room.
2. **Penetration** — the other person breaches the distance, usually by demonstrating either (a) vulnerability he is constitutionally compelled to protect (Kitty hunted by demons; Jubilee cornered in a mall; Rogue running) or (b) competence that earns wary respect (Jean's telepathic tact; Ororo's stillness; Mariko's refusal to be intimidated; Rogers' moral clarity).
3. **Idealization** — once the bond forms, it becomes near-religious. Mariko is not a woman but the gateway to being-a-man. Jean is not a colleague but the proof that he is *seeable*. Kitty is not a student but the daughter-self he could not save.
4. **Service** — he organizes his behavior around protecting the bond. This is his most regulated mode and produces his best functioning.
5. **Rupture** — the other person is endangered, taken, killed, turned, or revealed to have been a manipulation. Crucially, in the canonical cases *he is the proximate instrument* (Mariko poisoned, dies on his claws at her request, *Wolverine* vol. 2 #57; Jean dies repeatedly in his arms or by his necessity; the X-Men slaughtered by his hand under Mysterio's illusion in *Old Man Logan*; Itsu murdered while carrying his son; Rose impaled accidentally on his first extrusion).
6. **Withdrawal** — wilderness, alcohol, exile, the bar in the Yukon, the farm in California, the cabin nobody knows about, the rooftop alone.
7. **Reapproach** — usually compelled by a *new* vulnerable other requiring protection. The cycle restarts, transferred onto a fresh object.

The template is so consistent across writers — Wein, Claremont, Hama, Windsor-Smith, Miller, Millar, Aaron, Hickman — that it must be treated as constitutive of the subject rather than as a narrative tic. He cannot enter intimacy without already standing at the rupture step in his mind.

## 3. How He Bonds — The Behavioral Signature

Bond formation in this subject is **slow, somatic, and asymmetric**. He does not declare. He stations himself. The earliest signs are physical-spatial rather than verbal:

- He begins to *stand near* the person without speaking. In the Claremont mansion era, the observable datum is that he occupies the same rooms as Kitty Pryde for stretches of hours, neither initiating nor leaving — adjacent reading, adjacent training, a sentinel position.
- He begins to *track scent.* He knows, without needing to ask, when a bonded person is in the building, in distress, ovulating, ill, lying, frightened, or asleep. He does not announce this. It changes his posture.
- He gives *objects, not words.* A blade to Kitty (the Muramasa-blessed gift, eventually). A katana lesson to Jubilee. A nod to Rogers. A drink poured wordlessly across the bar.
- He performs *protective surveillance* — taking patrol shifts no one assigned him, walking a perimeter, sitting up the night a bonded person is sick or hunted.
- He *teaches survival skills he wishes had been taught to him.* This is the most reliable diagnostic that a bond has formed: the moment he begins to pedagogically transmit hard-won knowledge, the person has been internalized.

What he does *not* do: process aloud, narrate the relationship, ask for reciprocity, or tolerate sustained eye contact during emotional disclosure. The bond is built in the periphery of speech.

## 4. The Four Object-Classes — A Taxonomy of Intimacy

His relational world sorts cleanly into four classes, each with its own behavioral protocol.

### 4a. The Adolescent Ward (Kitty Pryde, Jubilee, Rogue, Armor, X-23, latterly the Krakoan young)

This is his **most regulated, most generative, and most durable** attachment zone. With adolescents — specifically female adolescents in or adjacent to lethal danger — the disorganized template *quiets*. The bond is non-sexual, fiercely protective, openly pedagogical, and characterized by an unusual capacity for sustained presence without flight.

Mechanism: the ward represents the child-self (himself at the moment of Rose's death, Laura at the moment of Facility activation) and the reparative project is to give *her* what no one gave *him* — survival training, a believer, a witness, and an adult who will not leave first. Because the relationship is structurally non-erotic, the Rose/Itsu/Mariko prediction ("she will die because of me") is partially short-circuited; the bond is permitted to exist.

Tells: he speaks more, but in shorter sentences; he tolerates touch (a hand on his arm from Kitty, a hug from Jubilee) that would otherwise produce withdrawal; he allows himself to be teased; he attends school recitals and birthdays; he answers the phone. With Laura specifically — the clone-daughter, the *one* opportunity to do fatherhood with full knowledge of what he is — he handles the role with comparative competence, ceding his own legacy (the Wolverine name, the mantle) to her in successive arcs.

### 4b. The Peer (Ororo Munroe, Kurt Wagner, Steve Rogers, Carol Danvers, Nightcrawler especially)

Peer bonds form by *demonstrated competence under shared fire* and are maintained by *codified ritual*: the chess game with Kurt, the rooftop cigar with Ororo, the parade-ground respect with Rogers, the wartime memory with Carol and Natasha. These relationships are characterized by **low verbal traffic and high mutual reliance**. He does not socialize with peers in unstructured leisure; he keeps appointments with them.

The peer bond tolerates long absences without degradation — he can vanish for a year and resume mid-sentence with Kurt. This is structurally important: peer bonds do not require him to remain present, which suits a man whose default response to relational pressure is geographic flight. They are *bonds that survive his withdrawal*, which makes them his safest intimate technology.

### 4c. The Romantic Object (Rose, Itsu, Mariko Yashida, Jean Grey, Silver Fox, Domino-class transients, Yukio as variant, latterly Storm/Domino arcs)

This is the **catastrophic zone**, and his behavior reflects accurate self-knowledge of it. With romantic objects he displays the most florid version of the approach-withdrawal cycle: ferocious idealization followed by sudden distance, then return, then loss. The load-bearing belief — *she will die because of me* — is not paranoid; it is empirically supported by his actual history (Rose, Itsu, Mariko all dead; Jean dead repeatedly and in part because of the Phoenix dynamics he could not arrest).

The pattern with Jean specifically is diagnostic. He could pursue and likely succeed; he does not, repeatedly. The conscious frame is "she's Scott's" — the operational reality is that *consummation would activate the kill-template*, and on some level he knows it. The unrequited frame keeps her alive in fantasy. When Phoenix forces a near-consummation (various crossover moments), his behavior decompensates immediately.

With Mariko the attempt at full integration is made — engagement, the *Wolverine* limited series structure of becoming-a-husband — and is destroyed by Mastermind's intervention and ultimately by her poisoning. He kills her himself at her request (Hama, *Wolverine* vol. 2 #57). After this the template is closed: he no longer attempts the marriage-form.

Sexual transients (the Madripoor "Patch" era, the bar pickups across decades) function as **affect-regulation behavior, not attachment-seeking**. They are categorized internally with alcohol and cigars: managed discharge of an internal state, with no expectation of continuity.

### 4d. The Adversary (Sabretooth, Romulus, the Hand collectively, Cyber, Omega Red, Daken in his hostile phase)

The most psychologically interesting category. His **most stable, longest-running relationship** is with the man who tries to murder him every birthday for a century. By any actuarial measure, Victor Creed has been more reliably present in his life than any lover, mentor, or friend. This is classical disorganized-attachment economics: the predator is the figure who *will not leave*, and presence is more important than valence to a system organized in early life around abandonment-by-violence.

The adversary bond is **ritualized, predictable, and oddly stabilizing**. He can locate Creed by scent across continents; he organizes his calendar around the birthday attempt; he refers to Creed in possessive terms ("my problem"); he has repeatedly declined opportunities to kill him permanently and decompensates on the occasions Creed is actually removed. Operationally, were Sabretooth permanently destroyed, the file predicts a destabilization event greater than any romantic loss to date.

The same logic governs his pre-Krakoan refusal to permanently end Daken, the Hand, or Romulus — the chronic antagonism is doing structural work he cannot consciously articulate.

## 5. How He Distrusts — The Default Posture

Distrust is the **resting state**, not a response. The justified premises are:

- Every institution that has ever owned his contract has installed a back door in his mind (Weapon X, Team X, Department H, the Hand, Hydra under Millar, the Apocalypse Death-Horseman overwrite, Persephone's resurrection triggers in the *Return* arc).
- His own memories are not reliable witnesses. He has been shown false biographies, false parents (the Romulus arc), false missions, and false friends (the Silver Fox/Team X memory complex).
- His own body has been used against people he loved without his consent (Mysterio's illusion in *Old Man Logan*; the Hand's possession in *Enemy of the State*).

The operational consequence is a **constant low-level interrogation protocol** he runs on every relationship: scent-checks for known handlers, perimeter scans on entering rooms, refusal to be sedated, refusal to be telepathically scanned without explicit prior trust, refusal to sleep in unsecured spaces. He has been observed (Claremont era) to sleep on floors, in closets, with his back to corners; in the Krakoan era this softens but does not disappear.

Trust is granted **incrementally and by class**. Xavier received conditional trust that was repeatedly tested and never fully closed (the Xavier Protocols / Onslaught revelation confirmed his suspicion). Rogers received unconditional trust, granted on pre-Weapon X data — Rogers is one of the only people whose moral credit predates the trauma. Jean received it. Kurt received it. Kitty received it the moment she demonstrated she would not be removed by his roughness. *No institution* has ever received it, and the Krakoan Quiet Council role is performed by him under explicit reservation, which the texts make clear.

## 6. How He Betrays — and the Asymmetry of It
