Each non-consensual resurrection is, behaviorally, a Weapon X re-enactment in slow motion: his body used by an institution to produce a version of himself he did not authorize. Expect cumulative damage on the autobiographical-trust axis, expect increased identification with the X-23 line (genetic continuance as a substitute for personal continuance), and expect, at the limit, a deliberate attempt to destroy the backup infrastructure itself.

---

## 3. The Open Questions — What the File Cannot Yet Answer

A surveillance file of this depth is obliged to mark its own ignorance. Six questions are genuinely undetermined by the existing record.

**Q1. Is the berserker state still trainable down, or is the neural pathway too consolidated?** A century of repetition argues it is now obligate under threshold conditions. But the Bushidō practice did reduce frequency in the late-Claremont period, and the post-Krakoan presentations show some episodes interrupted mid-cycle by deliberate intervention. The honest answer is: partially trainable, never extinguishable. A more interesting question: can a trusted other (Laura, Kurt, Ororo) be conditioned as an external regulator he will reliably accept input from in pre-threshold states? Limited evidence suggests yes for Kurt specifically; this is operationally useful.

**Q2. What is the actual ceiling of his autobiographical recovery?** Every "full restoration" has been partial. Is there a genuine bedrock of authentic Howlett-era memory that can in principle be reached, or is the whole stack — including the Origin material — itself a constructed narrative downstream of his dissociative architecture? The file cannot adjudicate this. The treatment implication, however, is the same in either case: see §2.3 — stop expecting recovery to be the cure.

**Q3. Daken.** The relationship with his biological son is the great unresolved file. Periodic rapprochements have failed; periodic attempted murders (in both directions) have failed to terminate it. The Daken bond does not fit the surrogate-daughter template (cleanly generative) or the Sabretooth template (cleanly hostile-stable). It is the one ongoing relationship in his life that has not stabilized into any pattern at all, which is diagnostically significant: it is the relationship his standard defenses do not handle. A genuine reconciliation here would be more therapeutically consequential than any other available move, *and* it is the move he is least equipped to make, because Daken is neither a child to protect nor an enemy to fight — he is an adult son demanding adult acknowledgment, which is exactly the relational register Logan has no template for.

**Q4. Long-horizon cognitive drift.** At 130+ chronological years with intact neural tissue and ongoing experiential load but compromised consolidation, what is the long-term cognitive profile? The healing factor protects against gross structural damage but cannot restore information that was never encoded or that was encoded under dissociated state. The file's working hypothesis: gradual narrowing of the autobiographical window to the last several decades, with the earlier century becoming increasingly mythologized rather than remembered. This is a normal aging pattern operating on an abnormally extended substrate. Behavioral consequence: increased reliance on persons who remember him from earlier periods (Creed, oddly, qualifies — another reason §2.2 matters).

**Q5. Is there a stable post-violence identity available to him at all?** The *Old Man Logan* experiment answers no — total inhibition produced depressive shutdown, not peace. But that experiment was conducted under maximum trauma load (the X-Men slaughter). The unanswered question is whether a *gradual, voluntary, supported* transition out of operational violence — over a decade or more, with mentorship roles, with Bushidō practice intensified, with the X-23 relationship as anchor — could produce a stable third option between operator and catatonic. The file is cautiously optimistic. The history is cautiously pessimistic. Bet line: even-money.

**Q6. The samurai ideal — recruitable to growth or fixed as shame?** The Bushidō frame is the most powerful organizing structure in his interior life. It currently functions primarily as a shame ledger (the standard against which he measures his failures). The open question is whether it can be re-recruited as a *forward* standard (the discipline through which the next several decades are constructed) rather than a *backward* judgment. Jasmine Falls remains psychologically live for him; a sustained return — months, not days — would be the natural site for this work.

---

## 4. The Catastrophe Envelope

The bounded set of outcomes that constitute genuine catastrophe — outcomes from which the subject does not return to baseline. Four pathways.

**4.1 The atrocity pathway.** A new compulsion attack (Hand-class, or a successor to Persephone's kill-trigger architecture) succeeds in producing a mass-casualty event against persons he is bonded to — a repeat of *Enemy of the State* or the *Old Man Logan* triggering event, but unambiguously real this time and not undoable by resurrection or retcon. Probability over the next decade: moderate, given the number of actors who have demonstrated the technical capacity. Consequence: full *Old Man* shutdown, terminal in the absence of a Laura-class anchor surviving and intervening.

**4.2 The anchor-loss pathway.** Simultaneous or near-simultaneous loss of two or more of his three principal anchors (samurai ideal, protector role, the X-23 / Laura line). Loss of any single anchor he has historically survived. Loss of two within a short window has not been tested and the file does not predict survival of intact identity through it.

**4.3 The resurrection-decoupling pathway.** Reliable institutional resurrection without his consent or with progressive fidelity drift across iterations, such that he comes to experience himself as a *series* of approximations rather than a continuous person. This is the slowest catastrophe and the hardest to detect from outside — the behavioral signature is increased fatalism, decreased investment in present relationships, and a flat affect in contexts that previously produced engagement. Adversaries cannot induce this; the institution he serves induces it, with good intentions.

**4.4 The terminal-attempt pathway.** Not "suicide" in the conventional sense — the lifelong low-grade wish for an ending is well-documented but has been chronically buffered by the protective role. If the protective role collapses (no children left to mentor, no team to anchor, Laura dead or estranged) and a method becomes available that the healing factor cannot reverse (the Muramasa blade, adamantium re-encasement, the specific configurations that have killed him before and might again), the probability of a deliberate walk into such a method is non-trivial. The file estimates this at low absolute probability but notes that the *conditions* for it have been more frequently satisfied in the post-resurrection era than in any prior period. This is the outcome the file most wishes to prevent and the one over which external intervention has the most leverage.

---

## 5. The Growth Envelope — What Pushes Toward Integration

Symmetrically, the inputs that move him toward genuine consolidation rather than continued cycling.

**5.1 Sustained relational falsification of the death-prediction.** Detailed in §2.1. Laura's continued life across decades, in close orbit, without termination by his hand or because of him, is the single most therapeutic possible input. Every additional year of her intact survival is direct evidence against the load-bearing belief.

**5.2 Reclaimed bodily sovereignty.** Detailed in §2.5. An explicit, honored, negotiated termination clause with the resurrection apparatus — even if never invoked — restores agency over the body that Weapon X took. The *possibility* of an ending is what makes continued life voluntary; voluntary life is the precondition of integrated life.

**5.3 Adult-register relationships.** Daken, but also: peer-to-peer friendships that do not depend on him being the protector. Kurt is the prototype; Ororo, episodically; Rogers, at moments. Expansion of this category — particularly to include any of the women he has historically idealized-then-withdrawn from, in a non-romantic adult-peer register — would loosen the rigidity of his relational repertoire.

**5.4 Re-recruitment of the samurai ideal as forward standard.** Detailed in §3, Q6. A sustained period at Jasmine Falls or its equivalent, with deliberate Bushidō practice as imposed structure for affect regulation, would be both regressive (returning to the inaugural site) and integrative (building forward from it). The historical evidence is that this practice works for him in proportion to the time invested.

**5.5 Surrender of the recovery project.** Detailed in §2.3. The day he stops trying to find out who he "really" is and starts answering the question with what he does next is the day his most exploitable vulnerability is closed. There are indications he has begun this work. He has not finished it.

**5.6 A successor.** The protective-mentor function is the cleanest part of him. Producing successors — Laura already operational, Gabby Kinney developing, the next generation of Xavier's students — institutionalizes the part of him that worked and outlives the parts that didn't. The samurai notion of the *student who carries the school* is available to him as frame. Investment here is high-yield and he knows it.

---

## 6. Operational Implications — Forecast Summary

For any party intending to *help* (the orientation of this dossier): the leverage points are Laura, Kurt, the Bushidō frame, and explicit resurrection-protocol negotiation. The interventions to avoid are anything that performs respect for him while ignoring his judgment, anything that places him on display as moral symbol, and anything that prolongs unstructured peace without a generative role embedded in it. Mentorship arrangements should be designed *for* him as much as for the students.

For any party intending to *break* him (the orientation this file exists to forestall): the historical record specifies the moves and the file declines to compile them in concentrated form. It is sufficient to note that the catastrophic pathways in §4 are not theoretical, that multiple actors have executed components of them, and that the subject is currently more vulnerable to the slow institutional pathway (§4.3) than to the acute pathways he has spent a century learning to survive.

The integrated forecast: a 60–70% probability of one or two more full cycles of the established loop within the next decade, terminating in re-stabilization at slightly degraded baseline; a 15–20% probability of a genuine integrative breakthrough driven by the Laura relationship and/or successful Bushidō re-investment; a 10–15% probability of entry into one of the catastrophe envelopes, with the resurrection-decoupling pathway the most probable of those and the atrocity pathway the most damaging. The subject's own probabilistic intuition about his own future is, on the available evidence, worse than this file's — he expects the catastrophe envelopes at substantially higher rates than the data warrant, which is itself a symptom of the condition under assessment and a leverage point for any clinician or comrade in a position to challenge it.

The final standing observation, which belongs in a forward assessment because it conditions every probability above: he has survived, intact enough to still be worth this file, through a century and a third of inputs that should have produced something far worse than what he is. The container holds. It was not designed to. He built it anyway, out of whatever was to hand — a dead girl's name, a teacher's etiquette, a series of borrowed daughters, a cigar, a code. That is the data point on which the growth envelope rests. A man who has improvised a self out of that little, that many times, retains the capacity to improvise one more.

## Relationship Graph
### Xavier
- Bedrock trust earned over decades despite Xavier's documented mind-edits of him.
- Failure mode: if Xavier is revealed (again) to have rewritten his memory or used him as an asset, regression to Weapon X-grade hostility — the lever an adversary would pull is documentary evidence of betrayal.
- Leverage: a personal request from Xavier moves him where institutional orders cannot.

### Rogers
- Pre-Weapon X friendship, mutual combat respect, the rare authority figure he doesn't insubordinate.
- Failure mode: a Rogers compromised, controlled, or revealed as morally fallen would destabilize a load-bearing internal reference — recent canon has tested this and it costs him.
- Leverage: Rogers can ask for the hard mission and get it.

### Jean
- Idealized-and-frustrated romantic axis; she is the canonical disconfirmation of his 'unfit' self-narrative, which is why he can't tolerate proximity to her for long.
- Failure mode: Phoenix-state Jean or Jean-in-mortal-danger collapses him into the Rose/Mariko configuration; he has killed her at her request before and the memory is load-bearing.
- Leverage: invoking Jean reaches him; threatening her or using her likeness is the kill-shot.

### Kitty Pryde
- First and template surrogate-daughter; pedagogical bond formed in the Kitty Pryde and Wolverine miniseries; the relationship that proved reparative parenting was possible for him.
- Failure mode: Kitty taken, tortured, or killed would trigger berserker beyond known threshold — Hand and Ogun have both pulled this lever.
- Leverage: she can call him back from places others can't reach.

### Jubilee
- Second-generation surrogate daughter; the bond that defined his 1990s solo run; later vampire-arc complications.
- Failure mode: Jubilee in danger overrides mission; Jubilee turned against him (vampire arc echoes) produces freeze, not violence — he won't strike her.
- Leverage: her safety is non-negotiable currency.

### Laura Kinney
- Clone-daughter; the one chance to do fatherhood without the Daken pattern; handled with comparative competence and visible tenderness.
- Failure mode: Laura's death or capture is a kill-shot configuration; Laura turned-by-trigger is the Weapon X mirror and may destabilize him below combat function.
- Leverage: Laura can ask anything.

### Sabretooth
- Century-long ritual adversarial pair-bond; annual birthday murder ritual; classic disorganized-attachment stable-hostile figure.
- Failure mode: Creed proximity degrades target discrimination by perimeter; paradoxically, Creed's permanent removal may be more destabilizing than his presence because the ritual is identity-organizing.
- Leverage: Creed's name in the wrong tone is enough to reroute his evening.

### Daken
- Son raised by enemies to hate him; the failed-fatherhood wound; the Itsu-template iterated forward.
- Failure mode: every interaction with Daken activates the Rose/Itsu shame ledger; manipulators have used Daken as bait and it works.
- Leverage: an adversary who can credibly threaten or use Daken owns a node Logan cannot rationalize past.

### Mariko Yashida
- The Bushidō-ideal romantic axis; the woman he killed at her request; ongoing internal interlocutor.
- Failure mode: her memory invoked manipulatively (a fake Mariko, a Mariko-coded woman in distress) lands harder than evidence should let it.
- Leverage: the samurai-ideal frame she represents recruits him.

### Kurt Nightcrawler
- Brother-bond, peer, the friend who reaches him in the kindest register he allows.
- Failure mode: Kurt's death has historically devastated him below working order; an adversary who knows this and can stage it has a heavy lever.
- Leverage: Kurt can ask the spiritual question and get an honest answer.

### Ororo Storm
- Peer, fellow leadership-skeptic, deep mutual respect.
- Failure mode: Ororo in command-conflict with him over a kid produces compliance, not rupture — but only with her.
- Leverage: she can override his exit cycle.

### [[Anna Marie LeBeau (Rogue)]]
- Surrogate-daughter and early teaching project; the Ms. Marvel personality-overlay arc cemented protective attachment.
- Failure mode: Rogue absorbed by an enemy creates a hostage-of-his-own-skill problem.
- Leverage: she calls him on the lies he tells himself.

### Romulus
- Long-running puppeteer figure; embodiment of the handler-class he most hates.
- Failure mode: any handler-coded figure can briefly reactivate the Romulus pattern.
- Leverage: revealing a Romulus-style hand behind a current event will redirect his entire agenda.

### Weapon X Personnel
- Cornelius, Hines, the Professor — the iatrogenic-trauma trio.
- Failure mode: scent or environmental cues alone (surgical light, antiseptic, the Weapon X facility hum) regress him to baseline arousal.
- Leverage: an adversary who reconstructs the Weapon X aesthetic owns the first thirty seconds of any engagement.
